These essential business functions must be performed to achieve Bus Operations’ mission. Each essential function, in turn, is supported by critical processes or services that are provided to the public or other departments within Metro. Essential functions are those that enable the department to provide vital services, maintain Metro’s good name, generate revenue, minimize legal exposure, protect life and property, or ensure the well-being of ridership and citizens.  A recovery time objective (RTO) is the amount of time in which systems, processes, services, or functions must be restored to acceptable levels to ensure the continuation of MEFs.  The following are MEFs for Bus Operations:  •	Facilities Maintenance & Bus Operations  o	Maintain bus communications.  o	Maintain non-revenue fleet.  o	Maintain revenue fleet.  o	Maintain HVAC system.  o	Maintain bus stops.  o	Fuel buses, non-revenue vehicles, and heavy-duty trucks.  •	Transportation  o	Operate Buses
2024 Rail Operations COOP Summary  Purpose and Scope  The Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority (Metro) developed this Continuity of Operations Plan (COOP) to ensure the continued execution of Mission Essential Functions (MEFs) during and after disruptive events. The plan aligns with federal and state guidelines, including NIMS, SEMS, and the California Government Code.  COOP Activation (Triggers)  The Continuity of Operations Plan (COOP) is activated when incidents disrupt Metro and Rail operations by impairing infrastructure, staffing, or technology for a significant period. Activation depends on whether the incident occurs with or without prior notice.  •	Incidents with Notice (e.g., severe weather, pandemics, planned events, labor strikes) allow for preparation and coordination among leadership, ensuring continuity measures are in place before disruptions occur.  •	Incidents without Notice (e.g., earthquakes, fires, power outages, terrorist events) require immediate response, often delaying activation due to assessment needs. Situational awareness from security, safety, and IT teams is critical in guiding response efforts.  The COOP Manager, in coordination with department leadership and Rail Operations Senior Leadership, oversees activation, communication, and operational continuity to minimize service disruptions.  Key Objectives  •	Ensure the continuity of essential rail services during emergencies.  •	Protect Metro’s facilities, assets, personnel, and infrastructure.  •	Minimize operational disruptions and financial losses.  •	Establish clear communication and coordination among Metro teams.  •	Support timely recovery and reconstitution of operations.  Mission Essential Functions (MEFs)  The following core functions must be maintained:  Rail Facilities Maintenance  •	Inspect and maintain stations, structures, and shop equipment  Rail Fleet Services  •	Inspect and maintain rail cars  •	Maintain Railcars for Revenue Service  •	Ensure Division and Shop Equipment Readiness  •	M3 Maintenance of records at all Divisions.    Continued on next page    Rail Transportation  •	Command and control of train movement  •	Move people via rail  Wayside Systems (Signals, Tracks, Power, Communications, SCADA, Wayside Systems)  •	Maintain tracks  •	Maintain Grade Crossings and Train Control system (Interlockings, Switches, Signals, Track Circuits, Cab Speed Network, Communication Network to SCADA  •	Maintain radio communication between trains and control center  •	Inspect and maintain third rail system, overhead catenary lines, substation, and all power in rail stations  •	Maintain SCADA system communications between Wayside Systems and Control Center  Phases of COOP Implementation  1.	Readiness & Preparedness: Identifying critical personnel, conducting training, and preparing facilities.  2.	Activation & Relocation: Mobilizing emergency response teams, assessing damage, and activating backup sites.  3.	Continuity Operations: Executing MEFs using alternate facilities or remote operations.  4.	Reconstitution & Recovery: Returning to normal operations, assessing response effectiveness, and implementing improvements.  Emergency Response  •	The COOP Manager oversees activation and coordination with Metro’s Emergency Management Department (EMD).  •	Incidents may require telework, facility relocation, devolution of authority, or temporary service suspension.  •	The Continuity Management Group (CMG) manages personnel assignments and recovery strategies.  Key Contacts During Emergencies:  •	Metro Employee Emergency Hotline: (877) 955-5234  •	Emergency Operations Center (EOC): (213) 922-8899  •	COOP Manager (Conan Cheung): (213) 418-3034    Authorized Activation Personnel  Position/Title 	Name	Office Phone:	Email:  Chief Operations Officer (COO)*	Conan Cheung	2134183034	CheungC@metro.net  Deputy COO	Edna Stanley	2139224084	StanleyE@metro.net  Deputy COO	Matthew Dake	2139224061	DakeM@metro.net  Deputy COO	Errol Taylor	2139223227	TayloeE@metro.net  *During incident response, the COO assumes the role of COOP Manager but may delegate this role to a Deputy COO if necessary.     heres a 2 page brief that is roughly a syllabus for a single class. Criteria for COOP Activation and Relocation Decisions  The COOP Manager or designated Rail personnel will activate the COOP in response to any of the incidents or situations based on the following criteria:    1.	The incident or situation will disrupt Metro operations and/or Rail operations by impairing infrastructure, staffing, or technology.  2.	The impairment will last for a considerable length of time.    The activation procedure depends on the amount of notification given, which greatly changes the ability to prepare, plan, and activate the COOP. The activation will be executed in one of two primary ways:  •	Incidents with notice  •	Incidents without notice       Incidents with notice include large-scale weather events, pandemics or biohazards, forewarned terrorist attacks, large-scale planned events such as conventions, sporting and cultural events, and labor strikes. Metro’s Emergency Management and other department executive leadership monitor these incidents with notice.    The COOP Manager communicates with department leadership about agency preparations and determines continuity actions in coordination with the Board, CEO, and designated Rail Personnel, and others as deemed necessary.    Leading up to such an event, all teams shall communicate actions, activities, conditions, and concerns to the COOP Manager, who will then funnel appropriate information to the Senior Leadership team (SLT) or Executive Staff.    The Rail Operations SLT is responsible for anticipating impacts and making decisions to manage and continue operations. The team leaders are fully responsible and accountable for managing operations throughout the Incident.  Incidents without notice are unplanned and generally unrelated to weather, such as major earthquakes, building fires, utility outages, disruptions, and breakdowns. Law enforcement and terrorist events often occur without notice. Incidents without notice do not allow time to consider possible impacts or activate planning and response procedures in advance. Many incidents without notice require immediate action by departments to reduce impacts to staff, facilities, and processes.    During the early stages of an incident without notice, accurate and timely situational awareness is vitally important. Situational awareness will usually be provided by various staff with expertise or proximity to the subject causing the impact. This may include security, building management, real estate, safety management, and information technology.    Initial response to an incident without notice may be delayed by the preliminary site assessment/investigation. Such an investigation can require time to determine the nature of the situation and the appropriate actions. Each incident is unique. import os  import docx    def extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path):  doc = docx.Document(docx_path)  sections = []  current_section = None  current_content = []  current_table_data = []    # Process paragraphs and headings  for para in doc.paragraphs:  # Check for headings (we assume all headings are section titles)  if para.style.name.startswith("Heading"):  # If there's an existing section, add it to sections  if current_section:  sections.append((current_section, current_content, current_table_data))  current_section = para.text.strip()  # Set new section title  current_content = []  # Reset content for the new section  current_table_data = []  # Reset table data for the new section  else:  # Regular content under the section  current_content.append(para.text.strip())    # Now process tables and add them to their respective section  for table in doc.tables:  table_row_data = []  for row in table.rows:  row_data = [cell.text.strip() for cell in row.cells]  table_row_data.append(" | ".join(row_data))  # Convert to Markdown table row    if table_row_data:  current_table_data.append(table_row_data)  # Store table data for current section    # Add the last section if exists  if current_section:  sections.append((current_section, current_content, current_table_data))    return sections    def sanitize_filename(name):  return name.replace(":", "_").replace("/", "_").replace("\\", "_")    def save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections):  if not os.path.exists(output_folder):  os.makedirs(output_folder)    for section, content, table_data in sections:  section_folder = os.path.join(output_folder, sanitize_filename(section))  os.makedirs(section_folder, exist_ok=True)    # Save the main section content in a .md file  section_filename = sanitize_filename(section) + ".md"  section_file_path = os.path.join(section_folder, section_filename)  with open(section_file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:  f.write("# " + section + "\n\n")  f.write("\n".join(content))    # Save each table in a separate .md file inside the section's folder  for idx, table in enumerate(table_data):  table_filename = f"table_{idx+1}.md"  table_file_path = os.path.join(section_folder, table_filename)  with open(table_file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:  f.write("**Table Data:**\n")  f.write("\n".join(table))  # Each table row is joined by newline    def process_docx(docx_path, output_folder):  sections = extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path)  save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections)  print(f"Processed and saved to {output_folder}")    # Example usage:  docx_file = r"L:\IV. Emergency Operations Plans (EOP)\Continuity Of Operations Plans (COOP)\2023-2024\BUS\2022 Bus Ops  COOP_DRAFT.docx"  output_dir = r"C:\Bus_Coop_Sectioned"  process_docx(docx_file, output_dir)  I've got this code that is close to what I want, but it creates a bunch of folders when I'd rather just have it dump all files into the output directory

import os    def replicate_folder_structure(source_dir, destination_dir):  """  Recursively replicates the folder structure from source_dir to destination_dir.  """  # Loop through the directory structure of the source folder    if os.name == "nt":  # Windows only  source_dir = f"\\\\?\\{source_dir}"  destination_dir = f"\\\\?\\{destination_dir}"    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(source_dir):  # Calculate the relative path of the current folder  relative_path = os.path.relpath(root, source_dir)    # Create the corresponding destination folder  destination_folder = os.path.join(destination_dir, relative_path)  if not os.path.exists(destination_folder):  os.makedirs(destination_folder)  print(f"Created folder: {destination_folder}")    # If you want to see the files, but we're not doing anything with them yet:  for file in files:  # You could optionally handle files here, but this script is only concerned with folders  pass    # Example usage:  source_path = r"L:"  # Replace with the actual path to your drive  destination_path = r"C:\Users\WeisburgC\OneDrive - Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority\Documents\coding messarounds\L_Copy"  # Replace with where you want the structure to be    # Make sure the destination path exists  if not os.path.exists(destination_path):  os.makedirs(destination_path)    # Call the function to replicate the folder structure  replicate_folder_structure(source_path, destination_path)  Is this right? import os  import shutil  import pypandoc  # Install with: pip install pypandoc    def convert_to_md(source_file, destination_file):  """Converts a file to Markdown format using Pandoc, if supported."""  try:  output = pypandoc.convert_file(source_file, 'markdown')  with open(destination_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:  f.write(output)  print(f"Converted: {source_file} -> {destination_file}")  except Exception as e:  print(f"Skipping {source_file} (Error: {e})")    def copy_and_convert_files(source_dir, destination_dir):  """  Copies all supported files from source_dir to destination_dir, converting them to .md.  """  source_dir = os.path.abspath(source_dir)  destination_dir = os.path.abspath(destination_dir)    # Apply \\?\ for long paths if on Windows  if os.name == "nt":  if not source_dir.startswith("\\\\?\\"):  source_dir = f"\\\\?\\{source_dir}"  if not destination_dir.startswith("\\\\?\\"):  destination_dir = f"\\\\?\\{destination_dir}"    for root, _, files in os.walk(source_dir):  # Get the relative path  relative_path = os.path.relpath(root, source_dir)  destination_folder = os.path.join(destination_dir, relative_path)    # Ensure the destination folder exists  os.makedirs(destination_folder, exist_ok=True)    for file in files:  source_file = os.path.join(root, file)    # Determine destination file name with .md extension  base_name, ext = os.path.splitext(file)  destination_file = os.path.join(destination_folder, base_name + ".md")    if ext.lower() in [".txt", ".pdf", ".docx", ".html"]:  # Supported formats  convert_to_md(source_file, destination_file)  else:  print(f"Skipping unsupported file: {source_file}")    # Example usage  source_path = r"C:\test1"  # Make sure it's correct  destination_path = r"C:\Users\WeisburgC\OneDrive - Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority\Documents\coding messarounds\L_Copy"    copy_and_convert_files(source_path, destination_path)   Can you modify this to do that?

def pdf_to_csv(pdf_path, csv_path):  """Extract text from the first page of a PDF and save it as a CSV file."""  try:  # Open the PDF file  doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)    # Extract text from the first page  if len(doc) > 0:  text = doc[0].get_text("text")  else:  print("PDF is empty.")  return    # Split text into lines  lines = text.split('\n')    # Write to CSV file  with open(csv_path, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as file:  writer = csv.writer(file)  for line in lines:  writer.writerow([line])  # Each line as a single column entry    print(f"CSV file saved at {csv_path}")  except Exception as e:  print(f"Error: {e}")    # Example usage  pdf_to_csv("\\metroshare01\EmergencyOperationsCenter\6. 2025 CURRENT EM EOC ACTIVITY\Wind and FireStorm 1.8.2025\SitReps\Wind and Fire Event Situation Report #009 1.10/25", "C:\Users\WeisburgC\OneDrive - Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority\Documents\coding messarounds\output.csv")  I'm getting some errors where fitz is not defined and csv is not defined

import fitz  # PyMuPDF import csv  def pdf_to_csv(pdf_path, csv_path): """Extract text from the first page of a PDF and save it as a CSV file.""" try: # Open the PDF file doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)  # Extract text from the first page if len(doc) > 0: text = doc[0].get_text("text") else: print("PDF is empty.") return  # Split text into lines lines = text.split('\n')  # Write to CSV file with open(csv_path, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as file: writer = csv.writer(file) for line in lines: writer.writerow([line])  # Each line as a single column entry  print(f"CSV file saved at {csv_path}") except Exception as e: print(f"Error: {e}")  # Example usage pdf_to_csv("input.pdf", "output.csv")   This code you gave me yesterday worked for one file if that helps

According to the release calendar specified in PEP 619, Python 3.10 is now in the "security fixes only" stage of its life cycle: 3.10 branch only accepts security fixes and releases of those are made irregularly in source-only form until October 2026. Python 3.10 isn't receiving regular bug fixes anymore, and binary installers are no longer provided for it. Python 3.10.11 was the last full bugfix release of Python 3.10 with binary installers.

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';    const MyComponent = () => {  // State to store screen width and height  const [screenSize, setScreenSize] = useState({  width: window.innerWidth,  height: window.innerHeight  });    // Update screenSize on window resize  useEffect(() => {  const handleResize = () => {  setScreenSize({  width: window.innerWidth,  height: window.innerHeight  });  };    // Event listener for window resize  window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);    // Clean up event listener on unmount  return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);  }, []);    // Use screen width and height to conditionally render  const isDesktop = screenSize.width >= 1024; // Adjust based on your desktop breakpoint  const isMobile = screenSize.width < 1024;  // Adjust based on your mobile breakpoint    return (  <main className="flex flex-row items-center justify-center w-full min-h-screen flex-1 px-8 gap-6 text-start">  {/* Conditional rendering based on screen size */}  {isDesktop && (  <div className="z-10 bg-opacity-0 relative flex flex-col min-h-screen h-full justify-center items-start">  {/* Desktop-specific content */}  </div>  )}    {isMobile && (  <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full px-4 py-10 z-10 bg-transparent flex justify-center items-center">  {/* Mobile-specific content */}  </div>  )}  </main>  );  };    export default MyComponent;   Actually reset. The three things I have genuine zeal for are patterns, puzzles, and people, and those interests are the reason I am applying for the Master’s of Science in Analytics program at the University of Southern California. I am an analytical explorer. I am naturally curious about the patterns in the world around me, especially when it comes to numbers and data and how those can be used to strategize and make informed decisions. Early in life, I was drawn to the beauty of activities like chess and music that required deep pattern recognition within a playful and low-stakes environment. Later, I was inspired by the real world application of patterns in business and the economy at large, thanks to books like Freakonomics by Steven Levitt and Stephen J. Dubner and Outliers by Malcolm Gladwell, as well as the light-hearted view of the dismal science portrayed by NPR’s Planet Money. These early influences led me to pursue mathematics and economics during my undergraduate degree. After college, I retained that playful curiosity of the analytical side of business in the many jobs I worked in, constantly asking my bosses questions about pricing, budgeting, and sales. However, the small businesses I worked for were not enough to scratch that pattern-loving itch in my soul, which is why I recently took an MIT summer course on machine learning and data analytics, and is why I am applying to the analytics program at USC. Later, I was inspired by the real world application of patterns in business and the economy at large, thanks to books like Freakonomics by Steven Levitt and Stephen J. Dubner and Outliers by Malcolm Gladwell, as well as the light-hearted view of the dismal science portrayed by NPR’s Planet Money. These early influences led me to pursue mathematics and economics during my undergraduate degree. After college, I retained that playful curiosity of the analytical side of business in the many jobs I worked in, constantly asking my bosses questions about pricing, budgeting, and sales. However, the small businesses I worked for were not enough to scratch that pattern-loving itch in my soul, which is why I recently took an MIT summer course on machine learning and data analytics, and is why I am applying to the analytics program at USC.  I am a complex problem solver who is energized by tricky puzzles. I find joy in discovering, creating, or reverse-engineering clever solutions. As early as I can remember, I was solving puzzles. Much of my childhood consisted of sudoku, rubik’s cubes, and jigsaw puzzles. To me, there is nothing more satisfying than finding a solution to a hard problem, which also led me to my interest in math. Even after college, I was always tinkering with puzzle design at the escape room or figuring out how to use a piece of recording equipment in music studios, and I even designed a working website for fun in an attempt to solve an organization problem for a previous boss. I think like an engineer that sees a real life problem and wants to solve it. It is that skill that draws me to the analytics program at USC.  I am a communicator. Some of my favorite times in creating music involve that special moment when I have an idea I think is really good and I have to start explaining it to others. I think that moment, where there is a theoretical intuition about something and it has to be put into words, is magical, and it takes real skill. I learned that just as well while tutoring in college. It is one thing for me to know how to solve a complicated calculus problem. It is entirely different, though just as exciting, for me to explain that solution to others in a way they understand. It is this passion of mine -the communication and collaboration between people- that I want to refine in the analytics program at USC.  I believe my combination of analytical insight, complex problem solving, and communication skills make me a strong applicant for this program, and I would love the opportunity to sharpen those skills at USC to make me an invaluable asset in the world beyond. I hope to use any resource gained during time at USC to make real contributions within society.  Can edit this? Don't change the content, but fix any grammar/ capitalization errors?

Before I became a career coach I was, at times, a job seeker. I was always a bit puzzled by the idea that I should “ask for the job” at the end of an interview. How would that sound? “Will you give me this job, please?” Laughable. Depending on the tone of voice, this could sound either like begging or an impatient whine! Then I imagined just bluntly saying, “I want this job.” Better, but abrupt. And what were they supposed to answer? “Oh, well, now that you ask, sure!” Yeah, right! A Pet Peeve of Interviewers: “I can’t tell whether he’s interested!” What it’s really about is this: at the end of any interview, the interviewer needs to know you’re seriously interested in moving forward in the process. If you’re not, they don’t want to waste time on further discussions. They can’t assume you’re interested just because you showed up for the interview. People often interview for jobs they’re not very interested in, either because the role might turn out to be better than it sounded in the posting, or even just for practice. If this is the final interview before consideration of an offer, they need to know you want the job. Even if you’re still not sure the salary or specifics are going meet your requirements, if the job itself is something you’d like to do, say so. The rest can often be negotiated. How to Ask for the Job: Examples This is how asking for the job might sound. •	“Based on everything I’ve heard and seen, it’s pretty clear to me that I want this job. With my strategic planning and team building skills, I can really see myself helping this program grow to its potential.” •	“I know you have a process so I won’t expect an answer right now, but I’d really like to join your team. Please let me know if you need anything else from me.” •	“I want you to know that I’m very interested in taking on this role, and I hope you’ll be making me an offer. Thanks again for meeting with me.” You may have heard of bolder ways of asking, like “So, have I got the job?” In sales an approach like this may be called for in order to demonstrate your aggressive sales closing technique, but for most roles a gentler statement like those above is best, in order to avoid putting the interviewer on the spot. A Solvable Problem: Fearing What You’ll Hear Job seekers are quite understandably anxious about sticking their necks out by asking for the job. If you ask yourself why, you may notice that you’re worried about what you’ll hear in response. So let’s get you prepared for the possibilities. First, it’s highly unlikely that they’re going to say no right on the spot. If this did happen you could say calmly, “Well, that’s a bit of a surprise.” (Smile.) “I’m interested in knowing your reasons for that decision.” The much more likely response is: “That’s good to know, because we’re very interested in you as well, and we’ll get back to you within the next (few days, couple of weeks, etc.).” You then say something like “Great!” Pretty do-able, really. Now remember, you’re not a mind reader. Decide right now that whatever they say, you’ll accept it with an open mind and a confident smile. Practice that in your mind, or even in a mirror. After you’ve done that you may find that you’re feeling less shy about saying you want the job. I hope the above gives you a more workable view of how to ask for the job at the end of your job interviews. For more tips, read my post on what to say at the end of the interview. I just did a test preparing for the GRE. Can you give me feedback on my essay?
Prompt::: All too often, companies hire outside consultants to suggest ways for the company to operate more efficiently. If companies were to spend more time listening to their own employees, such consultants would be unnecessary. Write a response in which you discuss the extent to which you agree or disagree with these statements and explain your reasoning for the position you take. In developing and supporting your position, you should consider ways in which the statements might or might not hold true and explain how these considerations shape your position.   Response::: When a business hires an outside consultant for advice regarding operations, employees may feel disgruntled because they believe they know the business and possible inefficiencies better than any outside source. However, independent help offers a unique perspective and role that does provide an important and valuable service to businesses because they may have wider experience within an industry, they have the right incentive structure, and they have a wider knowledge for tools that a business could use to become more efficient. Consultants have worked with many business, often within the same industry, and they can provide insight to how other businesses are working well. When a consultant is moving quickly between businesses, they get this unique perspective of what is happening on a larger scale and know what sort of trends and improvements are being made on the wider scale. Employees may know the individual business better, but an outside consultant knows the industry better. Consider a young entrepreneur that is forming a business within the landscaping industry. The advivce that he needs to grow the business will not lie within his employees who are cutting grass and planting bushes all day. He needs help from someone older and more experienced within the industry- someone who understands the sales process better or may have tips on where to find cheaper supplies. Some of that knowledge may lie within the employees too, but it is far likelier to be within someone that has tested the advice and struggled through the same things. Consultants are also important because their incentives are aligned in the right way. Someone within the company is paid to do a certain role, perhaps to fix irragation systems. That person may notice ways that the business might function better, but often there is no incentive for that person to actually fix the problem. They are paid the same whether they fix the problem or not. However, a consultant is paid to find and solve those problems. The consultant has the right incentive to address problems within a company. Finally, consultants have access to a wider knowledge of tools available to businesses. If there is an issue with the scheduling system for a service company, employees may not know of any other options, but a consultant might. Consultants are very useful to businesses.

 try {  const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);  const pool = await poolPromise;  await pool.request()  .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)  .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)  .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');  res.redirect('/login');  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');  }  });    // User login route  app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {  const { username, password } = req.body;  try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  const result = await pool.request()  .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)  .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');  if (result.recordset.length > 0) {  const user = result.recordset[0];  const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);  if (passwordMatch) {  const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);  req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session  res.cookie('authToken', token);  res.redirect('/bubbles');  } else {  res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');  }  } else {  res.status(400).send('User not found.');  }  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);    app.get('/', (req, res) => {  res.redirect('/login'); // Redirects root URL to the login page  });    // User registration route  app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {  const { username, password } = req.body;  try {  const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);  const pool = await poolPromise;  await pool.request()  .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)  .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)  .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');  res.redirect('/login');  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');  }  });  app.get('/clear-sessions', (req, res) => {  req.sessionStore.all((err, sessions) => {  if (err) {  return res.status(500).send('Error clearing sessions.');  }    // Iterate through all sessions and destroy them  for (let sessionId in sessions) {  req.sessionStore.destroy(sessionId, (err) => {  if (err) {  console.error(`Failed to destroy session ${sessionId}:`, err);  }  });  }    res.send('All sessions cleared.');  });  });  // User login route  app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {  const { username, password } = req.body;  try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  const result = await pool.request()  .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)  .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');  if (result.recordset.length > 0) {  const user = result.recordset[0];  const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);  if (passwordMatch) {  const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);  req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session  res.cookie('authToken', token);  res.redirect('/bubbles');  } else {  res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');  }  } else {  res.status(400).send('User not found.');  }  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).send('Login failed.');  }  });    // Route to serve the bubble site after login  app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {  const token = req.cookies.authToken;  if (token) {  try {  jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.redirect('/login');  }  } else {  res.redirect('/login');  }  });    // Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database  app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects  console.log(userId, bubbles);    if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {  return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });  }    try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)  await pool.request()  .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)  .query('DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');    // Insert each bubble into the database  for (const bubble of bubbles) {  const { group, text } = bubble;  await pool.request()  .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)  .input('text', sql.NVarChar, text)  .input('group', sql.NVarChar, group)  .query('INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)');  }    res.json({ success: true });  } catch (error) {  console.error("Database error:", error);  res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });  }  });    // Endpoint to load user's bubbles  app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {  const token = req.cookies.authToken;  if (token) {  try {  const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);  const userId = decoded.id; // Assuming userId is included in your token  const pool = await poolPromise;  const bubblesResult = await pool.request()  .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)  .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');    res.json({  success: true,  bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the user's bubbles  });  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });  }  } else {  res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });  }  });    // Serve the login page  app.get('/login', (req, res) => {  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));  });    // Route to retrieve and print Users table  app.get('/users', async (req, res) => {  try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  const result = await pool.request().query('SELECT * FROM Users');  console.log(result.recordset);  res.json(result.recordset);  } catch (error) {  console.error("Database error:", error);  res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });  }  });    // Route to retrieve all bubbles associated with user with id=3  app.get('/userbubbles', async (req, res) => {  const userId = 3; function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {  textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {  const inputField = document.createElement('input');  inputField.type = 'text';  inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text  textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field  inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input    inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {  updateText();  });    // Listen for the Enter key  inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {  if (event.key === 'Enter') {  updateText();  }  });    function updateText() {  textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value  inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text  }  });  }

function makeBubbleDraggable(bubble) {  bubble.addEventListener('mousedown', function (event) {  offsetX = event.clientX - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().left; // Calculate horizontal offset  offsetY = event.clientY - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().top; // Calculate vertical offset    function mouseMoveHandler(e) {  bubble.style.position = 'absolute'; // Set position to absolute  bubble.style.left = `${e.clientX - offsetX}px`; // Use the offset  bubble.style.top = `${e.clientY - offsetY}px`; // Use the offset  }    function mouseUpHandler() {  document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);  document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);  }    document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);  document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);  });  }

const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');  const createBubbleBtn = document.getElementById('create-bubble');    const groups = {}; // Object to hold groups    function getRandomColor() {  const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';  let color = '#';  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {  color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];  }  return color;  }  function getGroupPosition(group) {  return group.getBoundingClientRect(); // Get the current position and size of the group  }  function createGroup(name, color) {  const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');  groupDiv.classList.add('group');  groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`; // Set border color  groupDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent'; // No fill  groupDiv.style.padding = '10px'; // Add some padding  groupDiv.style.margin = '10px'; // Add some margin for spacing    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');  groupTitle.innerText = name;  groupTitle.style.marginBottom = '10px'; // Add some space below the title  groupDiv.appendChild(groupTitle);    // Only align bubbles if there are already bubbles in the group      return groupDiv; // Return the group element  }    function createBubble() {  const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();  if (!groupName) return;    let group = groups[groupName];    if (!group) {  const color = getRandomColor(); // Generate a new color for the group  group = createGroup(groupName, color);  groups[groupName] = group; // Store the group in the groups object  document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group); // Add the group to the container  }    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');  newBubble.classList.add('bubble');  newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.style.borderColor; // Set the bubble color  newBubble.style.width = '50px';  newBubble.style.height = '50px';  newBubble.style.borderRadius = '10px'; // Rounded corners  newBubble.style.margin = '5px'; // Spacing between bubbles  newBubble.style.position = 'absolute'; // Ensure bubbles can be positioned  newBubble.style.cursor = 'move'; // Change cursor to indicate draggable    // Set a random initial position for the bubble  newBubble.style.left = `${Math.random() * (window.innerWidth - 50)}px`; // Random position  newBubble.style.top = `${Math.random() * (window.innerHeight - 50)}px`; // Random position    // Create a span for editable text  const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit"; // Default text  textSpan.style.display = 'block'; // Display block for line breaks  textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center'; // Center text    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan); // Add the text span to the bubble  document.body.appendChild(newBubble); // Append bubble to body for free movement    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; // Store the group name in a data attribute  group.bubbles.push(newBubble); // Ensure this line is executed  group.element.appendChild(newBubble); // Ensure bubbles are added to the correct group    // Make the bubble editable  makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);    // Call functions for dragging  makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);  console.log(JSON.stringify(groups, null, 2));  callBack([...document.querySelectorAll('.group')]);  }    function callBack() {  Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {  const group = groups[groupName];  const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the new position of the group    group.bubbles.forEach(bubble => {  // Move each bubble to align with the new group position  moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition);  });  });  }    function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition) {  bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + 20}px`; // Example positioning logic  bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + 50}px`; // Example positioning logic  }    function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {  textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {  const inputField = document.createElement('input');  inputField.type = 'text';  inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text  textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field  inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input    inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {  updateText();  });    // Listen for the Enter key  inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {  if (event.key === 'Enter') {  updateText();  }  });    function updateText() {  textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value  inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text  }  });  }    function makeBubbleDraggable(bubble) {  let offsetX, offsetY;    bubble.addEventListener('mousedown', function (event) {  offsetX = event.clientX - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().left; // Calculate horizontal offset  offsetY = event.clientY - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().top; // Calculate vertical offset    // Bring the bubble to the front when dragging  bubble.style.zIndex = 1000;    function mouseMoveHandler(e) {  bubble.style.left = `${e.clientX - offsetX}px`; // Use the offset  bubble.style.top = `${e.clientY - offsetY}px`; // Use the offset  }    function mouseUpHandler() {  // Stop listening for the dragging events  document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);  document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);    // Call the callback function after dragging ends  callBack(); // This can snap the bubble back to its group if needed    // Reset z-index when done dragging  bubble.style.zIndex = '';  }    document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);  document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);  });  }            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {  document.getElementById('create-bubble').addEventListener('click', createBubble);    // Add keyboard event listener for Ctrl + B  document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {  if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'b') {  e.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default browser action  createBubble(); // Call createBubble function  }  });  });

<!DOCTYPE html>  <html lang="en">  <head>  <meta charset="UTF-8">  <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">  <title>Interactive Bubbles</title>  <link rel="stylesheet" href="styles.css">  </head>  <body>  <button id="create-bubble">Create Bubble</button>   <button id="delete-group">Delete Group</button>  <div id="bubble-container" class="grid-container"></div>      <script src="script.js"></script>  </body>  </html>  const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');  const createBubbleBtn = document.getElementById('create-bubble');    const groups = {}; // Object to hold groups    function getRandomColor() {  const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';  let color = '#';  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {  color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];  }  return color;  }  function getGroupPosition(group) {  return group.getBoundingClientRect(); // Get the current position and size of the group  }  function createGroup(name, color) {  const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');  groupDiv.classList.add('group');  groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`;  groupDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';  groupDiv.style.padding = '10px';  groupDiv.style.margin = '10px';    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');  groupTitle.innerText = name;  groupDiv.appendChild(groupTitle);    // Return an object with the group element and an empty bubbles array  return { element: groupDiv, bubbles: [] };  }    function deleteGroup(groupName) {  const group = groups[groupName]; // Find the group in the groups object    if (!group) {  alert(`Group '${groupName}' does not exist.`); // Show alert if the group is not found  return;  }    // Remove all bubbles in the group  group.bubbles.forEach(bubble => {  bubble.remove(); // Remove the bubble from the DOM  });    // Remove the group element from the DOM  group.element.remove();    // Remove the group from the `groups` object  delete groups[groupName];    callBack();    console.log(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`);  alert(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`); // Show success message  }    function createBubble() {  const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();  if (!groupName) return;    let group = groups[groupName];    if (!group) {  const color = getRandomColor();  group = createGroup(groupName, color);  groups[groupName] = group;  document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element);  callBack();  }    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');  newBubble.classList.add('bubble');  newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor;    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';  newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';  newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the group's position  const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20; // Position relative to the group  const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50; // Position relative to the group  newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group  newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group  newBubble.style.zIndex = 1; // Initial z-index for bubbles    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";  textSpan.style.display = 'block';  textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);  document.body.appendChild(newBubble);    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName;  group.bubbles.push(newBubble);    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);  makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);  callBack();  }      function callBack() {  Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {  const group = groups[groupName];  const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);    group.bubbles.forEach((bubble, index) => {  moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index);  });  });  }    function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index) {  const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble  const bubbleHeight = bubble.offsetHeight; // Get the current height of the bubble  const marginTop = 60; // Space for the group title  const spacing = 10; // Space between bubbles    // Calculate the left position for the bubble  const leftPosition = groupPosition.left + (bubbleWidth + spacing) * (index % Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing)));    // Calculate the top position for the bubble  const topPosition = groupPosition.top + marginTop + Math.floor(index / Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing))) * (bubbleHeight + spacing);    bubble.style.left = `${leftPosition}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${topPosition}px`;    // Calculate how many bubbles can fit in a row  const bubblesPerRow = Math.floor((groupPosition.width) / (bubbleWidth + spacing));    // Calculate the x position to center bubbles  const offsetX = (groupPosition.width - (bubblesPerRow * (bubbleWidth + spacing) - spacing)) / 2;    // Calculate the x and y positions  const xPosition = offsetX + (index % bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleWidth + spacing);  const yPosition = Math.floor(index / bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleHeight + spacing) + marginTop;    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + xPosition}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + yPosition}px`;  }      function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {  textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {  const inputField = document.createElement('input');  inputField.type = 'text';  inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text  textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field  inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input    inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {  updateText();  });    // Listen for the Enter key  inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {  if (event.key === 'Enter') {  updateText();  }  });    function updateText() {  textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value  inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text  }  });  }    function makeBubbleDraggable(bubble) {  let offsetX, offsetY, originalGroup;    bubble.addEventListener('mousedown', function (event) {  offsetX = event.clientX - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().left;  offsetY = event.clientY - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().top;  originalGroup = bubble.dataset.group; // Store the original group    // Bring the bubble to the front when dragging  bubble.style.zIndex = 1000;    function mouseMoveHandler(e) {  bubble.style.left = `${e.clientX - offsetX}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${e.clientY - offsetY}px`;  }    function mouseUpHandler(e) {  // Stop listening for dragging events  document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);  document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);    // Check for the group where the bubble is released  const newGroupElement = document.elementFromPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY);    if (newGroupElement && newGroupElement.classList.contains('group')) {  const newGroupName = newGroupElement.querySelector('h3').innerText.trim().toLowerCase(); // Get the group name    // If the bubble is dropped in a different group  if (newGroupName !== originalGroup) {  // Remove the bubble from the original group  const originalGroupElement = groups[originalGroup].element;  originalGroupElement.removeChild(bubble); // Ensure this is the correct element    // Append the bubble to the new group  newGroupElement.appendChild(bubble);  bubble.dataset.group = newGroupName; // Update the group data attribute  }  }    // Reset z-index when done dragging  bubble.style.zIndex = '';  }    document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);  document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);  });  }                          document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {  document.getElementById('create-bubble').addEventListener('click', createBubble);    // Add keyboard event listener for Ctrl + B  document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {  if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'b') {  e.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default browser action  createBubble(); // Call createBubble function  }  });  });        document.getElementById('delete-group').addEventListener('click', function () {  const groupName = prompt("Enter the name of the group you want to delete:").trim().toLowerCase();    if (!groupName) return; // If the input is empty or cancelled, do nothing    deleteGroup(groupName); // Call deleteGroup function with the group name  });      // Create a custom context menu  const contextMenu = document.createElement('div');  contextMenu.style.position = 'absolute';  contextMenu.style.display = 'none';  contextMenu.style.backgroundColor = '#fff';  contextMenu.style.border = '1px solid #ccc';  contextMenu.style.padding = '10px';  contextMenu.innerHTML = '<button id="delete-bubble-btn">Delete Bubble</button>';  contextMenu.style.zIndex = 5;    document.body.appendChild(contextMenu);    let targetBubble = null; // Variable to store the current bubble    // Function to show custom context menu  function showContextMenu(event, bubble) {  event.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default right-click menu  targetBubble = bubble; // Set the target bubble  contextMenu.style.left = `${event.pageX}px`;  contextMenu.style.top = `${event.pageY}px`;  contextMenu.style.display = 'block';  }    // Event listener for deleting the bubble  document.getElementById('delete-bubble-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {  if (targetBubble) {  targetBubble.remove(); // Delete the bubble  contextMenu.style.display = 'none'; // Hide the menu  }  });    // Hide context menu if clicked anywhere else  document.addEventListener('click', function() {  contextMenu.style.display = 'none';  });  #bubble-container {  position: relative;  /* Allows absolute positioning of bubbles */  width: 100vw;        /* Full width of the viewport */  height: 100vh;       /* Full height of the viewport */    background-color: #f0f0f0;  /* Optional: Background color for visibility */  margin-top: auto; /* Ensure bubbles appear below the title */  margin-bottom: auto; /* Center bubbles vertically between title and bottom */  }  .bubble {  padding: 10px;  /* Add some padding for better text visibility */  border-radius: 10px;  /* Rounded edges */    position: absolute;  cursor: pointer;  display: flex;  align-items: center;  justify-content: center;  text-align: center;  color: white;  font-size: 14px;  min-width: 150px;  /* Minimum width for consistency */  max-width: 200px;  /* Maximum width */  }    .bubble input {  width: 80%;  height: 20px;  text-align: center;  font-size: 14px;  }    .bubble-text {  cursor: pointer;  }      .grid-container {  display: grid;  grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(200px, 1fr)); /* Columns adjust to fit the screen */  grid-auto-rows: 1fr; /* Ensures rows take up equal vertical space */  gap: 10px; /* Space between grid items */  padding: 20px;  height: 100%; /* Full height of the parent container */  box-sizing: border-box;  }    .group {  border: 2px solid transparent;  background-color: transparent;  border-radius: 10px;  /* Rounded edges */  padding: 10px;  margin: 10px;  display: flex;  flex-direction: column;  justify-content: center; /* Center the bubbles vertically */  align-items: center; /* Center the bubbles horizontally */  height: 100%;  box-sizing: border-box;  position: relative; /* Allows title to stay at the top */  }    .group h3 {  text-align: center;  width: 100%;  margin: 0;  font-size: 30px;  font-size-adjust: .5;  padding-bottom: 10px;  position: absolute; /* Position the title at the top */  top: 0; /* Stick to the top */  left: 0;  right: 0; function makeBubbleDraggable(bubbleElement) {  let isDragging = false;  let offsetX, offsetY;    bubbleElement.addEventListener('mousedown', (event) => {  isDragging = true;  offsetX = event.clientX - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left;  offsetY = event.clientY - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;  bubbleElement.style.position = 'absolute';  });    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (event) => {  if (isDragging) {  bubbleElement.style.left = `${event.clientX - offsetX}px`;  bubbleElement.style.top = `${event.clientY - offsetY}px`;  }  });    document.addEventListener('mouseup', (event) => { // Pass event here  if (isDragging) {  isDragging = false;  // Check for collision with groups  Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {  const group = groups[groupName];  const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);  const groupRect = group.element.getBoundingClientRect();    // Check if the bubble is dropped within the group  if (  event.clientX >= groupRect.left &&  event.clientX <= groupRect.right &&  event.clientY >= groupRect.top &&  event.clientY <= groupRect.bottom  ) {  // Move the bubble to the new group  console.log(groupName)  changeBubbleGroup(bubbleElement, group);  }  });  }  });  }      function changeBubbleGroup(bubble, newGroup) {  // Assuming each bubble has a reference to its current group  const currentGroupName = bubble.currentGroup; // Adjust as per your structure    // Find the current group  const currentGroup = groups[currentGroupName];  const newGroupData = groups[newGroup];    if (!currentGroup || !newGroupData) {  console.error('Invalid group specified.');  return;  }    // Remove the bubble from the current group's child list  const bubbleIndex = currentGroup.bubbles.indexOf(bubble);  newGroupData.element.appendChild(bubble); // Add to DOM if necessary    // Update the bubble's current group reference  bubble.currentGroup = newGroup; // Adjust as per your bubble structure    console.log(`Moved bubble to group: ${newGroup}`); const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');  const createBubbleBtn = document.getElementById('create-bubble');    const groups = {}; // Object to hold groups    function getRandomColor() {  const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';  let color = '#';  for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {  color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];  }  return color;  }  function getGroupPosition(group) {  return group.getBoundingClientRect(); // Get the current position and size of the group  }  function createGroup(name, color) {  const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');  groupDiv.classList.add('group');  groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`;  groupDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';  groupDiv.style.padding = '10px';  groupDiv.style.margin = '10px';    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');  groupTitle.innerText = name;  groupDiv.appendChild(groupTitle);  console.log(groupDiv.children);  // Return an object with the group element and an empty bubbles array  return { element: groupDiv, bubbles: [] };  }    function deleteGroup(groupName) {  const group = groups[groupName]; // Find the group in the groups object    if (!group) {  alert(`Group '${groupName}' does not exist.`); // Show alert if the group is not found  return;  }    // Remove all bubbles in the group  group.bubbles.forEach(bubble => {  bubble.remove(); // Remove the bubble from the DOM  });    // Remove the group element from the DOM  group.element.remove();    // Remove the group from the `groups` object  delete groups[groupName];    callBack();    console.log(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`);  alert(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`); // Show success message  }    function createBubble() {  const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();  if (!groupName) return;    let group = groups[groupName];    if (!group) {  const color = getRandomColor();  group = createGroup(groupName, color);  groups[groupName] = group;  document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element);  callBack();  }    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');  newBubble.currentGroup = groupName;  console.log(newBubble.currentGroup);  newBubble.classList.add('bubble');  newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor;      newBubble.style.margin = '5px';  newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';  newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the group's position  const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20; // Position relative to the group  const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50; // Position relative to the group  newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group  newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group  newBubble.style.zIndex = 1; // Initial z-index for bubbles    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";  textSpan.style.display = 'block';  textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);  document.body.appendChild(newBubble);    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName;  group.bubbles.push(newBubble);    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);  makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);  callBack();    }      function callBack() {  Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {  const group = groups[groupName];  const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);  group.bubbles.forEach((bubble, index) => {  moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index);  });  });  }    function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index) {  const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble  const bubbleHeight = bubble.offsetHeight; // Get the current height of the bubble  const marginTop = 60; // Space for the group title  const spacing = 10; // Space between bubbles    // Calculate the left position for the bubble  const leftPosition = groupPosition.left + (bubbleWidth + spacing) * (index % Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing)));    // Calculate the top position for the bubble  const topPosition = groupPosition.top + marginTop + Math.floor(index / Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing))) * (bubbleHeight + spacing);    bubble.style.left = `${leftPosition}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${topPosition}px`;    // Calculate how many bubbles can fit in a row  const bubblesPerRow = Math.floor((groupPosition.width) / (bubbleWidth + spacing));    // Calculate the x position to center bubbles  const offsetX = (groupPosition.width - (bubblesPerRow * (bubbleWidth + spacing) - spacing)) / 2;    // Calculate the x and y positions  const xPosition = offsetX + (index % bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleWidth + spacing);  const yPosition = Math.floor(index / bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleHeight + spacing) + marginTop;    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + xPosition}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + yPosition}px`;  }      function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {  textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {  const inputField = document.createElement('input');  inputField.type = 'text';  inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text  textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field  inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input    inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {  updateText();  });    // Listen for the Enter key  inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {  if (event.key === 'Enter') {  updateText();  }  });    function updateText() {  textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value  inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text  }  });  }      function makeBubbleDraggable(bubbleElement) {  let isDragging = false;  let offsetX, offsetY;    bubbleElement.addEventListener('mousedown', (event) => {  isDragging = true;  offsetX = event.clientX - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left;  offsetY = event.clientY - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;  bubbleElement.style.position = 'absolute';  // Ensure it's positioned absolutely  });    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (event) => {  if (isDragging) {  console.log(bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left,bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top );  const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');  const containerRect = bubbleContainer.getBoundingClientRect();    bubbleElement.style.left = `${event.clientX - offsetX}px`;  bubbleElement.style.top = `${event.clientY -  offsetY}px`;  }  });    document.addEventListener('mouseup', (event) => {  if (isDragging) {  isDragging = false;    // Check for collision with groups  Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {  const group = groups[groupName];  const groupRect = group.element.getBoundingClientRect();    // Check if the bubble is dropped within the group  if (  event.clientX >= groupRect.left &&  event.clientX <= groupRect.right &&  event.clientY >= groupRect.top &&  event.clientY <= groupRect.bottom  ) {  changeBubbleGroup(bubbleElement, groupName, event.clientX, event.clientY); // Ensure groupName is passed correctly  }  });  }  });  }      function changeBubbleGroup(bubble, newGroupName, xdim, ydim) {  const currentGroupName = bubble.currentGroup;  const currentGroup = groups[currentGroupName];  const newGroup = groups[newGroupName];    if (!currentGroup || !newGroup) {  console.error('Invalid group specified.');  return;  }    // Get the bubble's current position before removing it  const bubbleRect = bubble.getBoundingClientRect();  const groupRect = newGroup.element.getBoundingClientRect();    // Calculate the offset of the bubble relative to the viewport  const offsetX = bubbleRect.left - window.scrollX; // Correct for window scroll  const offsetY = bubbleRect.top - window.scrollY;  // Correct for window scroll    // Remove the bubble from the current group's child list  const bubbleIndex = currentGroup.bubbles.indexOf(bubble);  if (bubbleIndex > -1) {  currentGroup.bubbles.splice(bubbleIndex, 1);  currentGroup.element.removeChild(bubble); // Ensure bubble is a child of currentGroup.element  }    // Add the bubble to the new group's child list  newGroup.bubbles.push(bubble);  newGroup.element.appendChild(bubble); // Add bubble to new group    // Set the bubble's position relative to the new group  // bubble.style.left = `${xdim}px`; // Adjust left position  // bubble.style.top = `${ydim}px`;   // Adjust top position    // Update the bubble's current group reference  bubble.currentGroup = newGroupName;    console.log(`Moved bubble to group: ${newGroupName}`);  }                            document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {  document.getElementById('create-bubble').addEventListener('click', createBubble);    // Add keyboard event listener for Ctrl + B  document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {  if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'b') {  e.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default browser action  createBubble(); // Call createBubble function  }  });  });        document.getElementById('delete-group').addEventListener('click', function () {  const groupName = prompt("Enter the name of the group you want to delete:").trim().toLowerCase();    if (!groupName) return; // If the input is empty or cancelled, do nothing    deleteGroup(groupName); // Call deleteGroup function with the group name  });      // Create a custom context menu  const contextMenu = document.createElement('div');  contextMenu.style.position = 'absolute';  contextMenu.style.display = 'none';  contextMenu.style.backgroundColor = '#fff';  contextMenu.style.border = '1px solid #ccc';  contextMenu.style.padding = '10px';  contextMenu.innerHTML = '<button id="delete-bubble-btn">Delete Bubble</button>';  contextMenu.style.zIndex = 5;    document.body.appendChild(contextMenu);    let targetBubble = null; // Variable to store the current bubble    // Function to show custom context menu  function showContextMenu(event, bubble) {  event.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default right-click menu  targetBubble = bubble; // Set the target bubble  contextMenu.style.left = `${event.pageX}px`;  contextMenu.style.top = `${event.pageY}px`;  contextMenu.style.display = 'block';  }    // Event listener for deleting the bubble  document.getElementById('delete-bubble-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {  if (targetBubble) {  targetBubble.remove(); // Delete the bubble  contextMenu.style.display = 'none'; // Hide the menu  }  });    // Hide context menu if clicked anywhere else  document.addEventListener('click', function() {  contextMenu.style.display = 'none';  });

Can you read how the text is being stored and help me access it better?  function createBubble() {  const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();  if (!groupName) return;    let group = groups[groupName];    // Create group if it doesn't exist  if (!group) {  const color = getRandomColor();  group = createGroup(groupName, color);  groups[groupName] = group;  document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element);  callBack();  }    // Create a new bubble  const newBubble = document.createElement('div');  newBubble.classList.add('bubble');  newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor;    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';  newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';  newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);  const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20;  const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50;  newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`;  newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`;  newBubble.style.zIndex = 1;    // Add editable text to the bubble  const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";  textSpan.style.display = 'block';  textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';  textSpan.style.zIndex = '10'; // Ensure the text span is on top and clickable    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);    const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');  bubbleContainer.appendChild(newBubble);    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName;  group.bubbles.push(newBubble);    // Add bubble edit and drag functionality  makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);  makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);    callBack();  }          function callBack() {  Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {  const group = groups[groupName];  const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);  group.bubbles.forEach((bubble, index) => {  moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index);  });  });  }    function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index) {  const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble  const bubbleHeight = bubble.offsetHeight; // Get the current height of the bubble  const marginTop = 60; // Space for the group title  const spacing = 10; // Space between bubbles    // Calculate the left position for the bubble  const leftPosition = groupPosition.left + (bubbleWidth + spacing) * (index % Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing)));    // Calculate the top position for the bubble  const topPosition = groupPosition.top + marginTop + Math.floor(index / Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing))) * (bubbleHeight + spacing);    bubble.style.left = `${leftPosition}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${topPosition}px`;    // Calculate how many bubbles can fit in a row  const bubblesPerRow = Math.floor((groupPosition.width) / (bubbleWidth + spacing));    // Calculate the x position to center bubbles  const offsetX = (groupPosition.width - (bubblesPerRow * (bubbleWidth + spacing) - spacing)) / 2;    // Calculate the x and y positions  const xPosition = offsetX + (index % bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleWidth + spacing);  const yPosition = Math.floor(index / bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleHeight + spacing) + marginTop;    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + xPosition}px`;  bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + yPosition}px`;    }      function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {  textSpan.addEventListener('click', function (event) {  event.stopPropagation();  // Prevent click events from affecting other elements    const inputField = document.createElement('input');  inputField.type = 'text';  inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  inputField.style.zIndex = '20';  // Ensure the input is on top    textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  inputField.focus();    // Disable dragging while editing  bubble.draggable = false;  inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {  setTimeout(() => {  updateText(inputField, bubble);  }, 0); // Delay by 0ms to ensure the 'keydown' event completes first  });    inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {  if (event.key === 'Enter') {  updateText(inputField, bubble);  }  });    });    function updateText(inputElement, bubble) {  const newValue = inputElement.value.trim();    if (newValue) {  const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = newValue;  textSpan.classList.add('bubble-text');    // Ensure the input element is still part of the DOM  if (inputElement.parentNode) {  inputElement.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Only replace if the input is still in the DOM  }    // Rebind the click event for editing  makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan);  }    // Enable dragging again  bubble.draggable = true;  }  }

 group = createGroup(groupName, color);  groups[groupName] = group;  document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element);  callBack();  }    // Create a new bubble  const newBubble = document.createElement('div');  newBubble.classList.add('bubble');  newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor;    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';  newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';  newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';  } function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {  textSpan.addEventListener('click', function (event) {  event.stopPropagation();  // Prevent click events from affecting other elements    const inputField = document.createElement('input');  inputField.type = 'text';  inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  inputField.style.zIndex = '20';  // Ensure the input is on top    textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  inputField.focus();    // Disable dragging while editing  bubble.draggable = false;  inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {  setTimeout(() => {  updateText(inputField, bubble);  }, 0); // Delay by 0ms to ensure the 'keydown' event completes first  });    inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {  if (event.key === 'Enter') {  updateText(inputField, bubble);  }  });    });    function updateText(inputElement, bubble) {  const newValue = inputElement.value.trim();    if (newValue) {  const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = newValue;  textSpan.classList.add('bubble-text');    // Ensure the input element is still part of the DOM  if (inputElement.parentNode) {  inputElement.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Only replace if the input is still in the DOM  }    // Rebind the click event for editing  makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan);  }    // Enable dragging again  bubble.draggable = true;  }  }  So when a bubble is initialized originally, the 'click to edit' text is not saved in the DOM in the same way.  }  });    });    function updateText(inputElement, bubble) {  const newValue = inputElement.value.trim();    if (newValue) {  const textSpan = document.createElement('span');  textSpan.innerText = newValue;  }    // Enable dragging again  bubble.draggable = true;  }  }      function makeBubbleDraggable(bubbleElement) {  let isDragging = false;  let offsetX, offsetY;    bubbleElement.addEventListener('mousedown', (event) => {  isDragging = true;  offsetX = event.clientX - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left;  offsetY = event.clientY - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;  bubbleElement.style.position = 'absolute';  // Ensure it's positioned absolutely  });    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (event) => {  if (isDragging) {  // console.log(bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left,bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top );  const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
