const express = require('express');  const session = require('express-session');  const sql = require('mssql');  const path = require('path');  const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');  const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');  const cookieParser = require('cookie-parser');    const app = express();    // Middleware for handling POST data  app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));  app.use(express.json());  app.use(cookieParser()); // Middleware to parse cookies    // Serve static files from bubbleSiteFiles directory  app.use('/bubbles', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles')));    require('dotenv').config();    // SQL Server configuration  const poolConfig = {  user: process.env.DB_USER,              // Use environment variable  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,      // Use environment variable  server: process.env.DB_SERVER,          // Use environment variable  database: process.env.DB_DATABASE,      // Use environment variable  options: {  encrypt: true, // Set to true if using Azure  trustServerCertificate: false, // Set to true for local testing, if necessary  enableArithAbort: true, // Required for Azure SQL  },  };    // JWT secret key  const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET; // Use environment variable    // Create a connection pool  const poolPromise = new sql.ConnectionPool(poolConfig)  .connect()  .then(pool => {  console.log('Connected to MSSQL');  return pool;  })  .catch(err => {  console.error('Database connection failed: ', err);  });      // Session middleware setup  app.use(session({  secret: JWT_SECRET, // Replace with your secret key  resave: false,  saveUninitialized: true,  cookie: { secure: false } // Set to true if using HTTPS  }));    app.get('/', (req, res) => {  res.redirect('/login'); // Redirects root URL to the login page  });    // User registration route  app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {  const { username, password } = req.body;  try {  const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);  const pool = await poolPromise;  await pool.request()  .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)  .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)  .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');  res.redirect('/login');  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');  }  });    // User login route  app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {  const { username, password } = req.body;  try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  const result = await pool.request()  .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)  .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');  if (result.recordset.length > 0) {  const user = result.recordset[0];  const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);  if (passwordMatch) {  const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);  req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session  res.cookie('authToken', token);  res.redirect('/bubbles');  } else {  res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');  }  } else {  res.status(400).send('User not found.');  }  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).send('Login failed.');  }  });    // Route to serve the bubble site after login  app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {  const token = req.cookies.authToken;  if (token) {  try {  jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.redirect('/login');  }  } else {  res.redirect('/login');  }  });    // Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database  app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects  console.log(userId, bubbles);    if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {  return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });  }    try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)  await pool.request()  .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)  .query('DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');    // Insert each bubble into the database  for (const bubble of bubbles) {  const { group, text } = bubble;  await pool.request()  .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)  .input('text', sql.NVarChar, text)  .input('group', sql.NVarChar, group)  .query('INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)');  }    res.json({ success: true });  } catch (error) {  console.error("Database error:", error);  res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });  }  });    // Endpoint to load user's bubbles  app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {  const token = req.cookies.authToken;  if (token) {  try {  const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);  const userId = decoded.id; // Assuming userId is included in your token  const pool = await poolPromise;  const bubblesResult = await pool.request()  .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)  .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');    res.json({  success: true,  bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the user's bubbles  });  } catch (err) {  console.error(err);  res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });  }  } else {  res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });  }  });    // Serve the login page  app.get('/login', (req, res) => {  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));  });    // Route to retrieve and print Users table  app.get('/users', async (req, res) => {  try {  const pool = await poolPromise;  const result = await pool.request().query('SELECT * FROM Users');  console.log(result.recordset);  res.json(result.recordset);  } catch (error) {  console.error("Database error:", error);  res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });  }  });    // Route to retrieve all bubbles associated with user with id=3  app.get('/userbubbles', async (req, res) => {  const userId = 3;
